  [33mΓÜá[39m [33mBugs: Missing effect dependencies[39m
    [36mLearn more: https://www.react.doctor/docs/rules/react-doctor/exhaustive-deps[39m
[2m    ΓåÆ Don't blindly add missing dependencies. Read the hook[22m
[2m    callback first.[22m
[2m    [22m
[2m    Bad:[22m
[2m    useEffect(() => {[22m
[2m      setCount(count + 1);[22m
[2m    }, [count]);[22m
[2m    [22m
[2m    Better:[22m
[2m    useEffect(() => {[22m
[2m      setCount((currentCount) => currentCount + 1);[22m
[2m    }, []);[22m
[2m    [22m
[2m    If the missing value is recreated every render, move it[22m
[2m    inside the hook or stabilize it before adding it to deps.[22m
